FROM (
    SELECT `p`.`Id`, `p`.`Attack`, `p`.`CryUrl`, `p`.`Defense`, `p`.`Description`, `p`.`HP`, `p`.`ImageUrl`, `p`.`Name`, `p`.`SpAttack`, `p`.`SpDefense`, `p`.`Speed`
    FROM `Pokemons` AS `p`
    WHERE `p`.`Id` = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS `t`
LEFT JOIN `PokemonTypes` AS `p0` ON `t`.`Id` = `p0`.`PokemonId`
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT `p1`.`Id`, `p1`.`MoveId`, `p1`.`PokemonId`, `m`.`Id` AS `Id0`, `m`.`Accuracy`, `m`.`Name`, `m`.`PP`, `m`.`Power`, `m`.`TypeName`

) AS `t`
